###SECRET RELIGION TRAITS###

		secretly_zun_pagan
		secretly_zun_pagan_reformed
		secretly_hellenic_pagan
		secretly_pagan
	}

	is_visible = {
		OR = {
			character = FROM
			society_member_of = secret_religious_society_aquileian
			AND = {
				is_close_relative = FROM
				trait = secretly_aquileian
			}
		}
	}
	
	same_opinion = 15

	random = no
	customizer = no
	ai_zeal = -50
}
